< Text>
When it comes to tacos, I pull out all the stops! I love tacos! I found this little spot entering Farmersville. The prices are great. The meats are tasty; especially the carnitas and lengua. I suggest eating tacos on site because the tortillas got rough around the edges when I brought them home. I also loved the grilled jalapenos and chopped onion (though I favor a spicy chile). I recommend this so for any taco lover.</Text>

When I went in for my appointment the stylist and I went over what I wanted to get done. I showed her various pictures and I made sure she was aware of my previous hair color history and that we were on the same page. She seemed to understand what I wanted to have done and quoted me at $230. I've been to higher end salons so the price wasn't too surprising to me except that this salon is not a high end salon. The salon is small and has about 10 stations with 4 shampoo chairs. Now here is what went wrong during my visit as she was drying my hair I noticed how warm toned it looked. The only difference I had was that the highlight placement was simply higher and and it now looked like I had an ombr√©! Scary I know, I asked the stylist if she could add some dark pieces in order to break up what looked like an ombr√© and so that it would add some sort of dimension. Being dissatisfied and unhappy I let her add the dark pieces throughout my hair just so I could feel comfortable to go out in public and go to work. <name>Rodney S<//name>< Review>
Foodie Fozzy says "WaBa, WaBa, WaBa!!"

Looking for another place to eat & review, a hot & humid Saturday had us stopping by the nearest newly opened WaBa Grill in Lakewood.

Clean, modern-looking d√©cor with ample table seating is what my eyes spied as I first walked in.  Loved the refreshing full blast A/C to cool off on a sweltering day.  Perusing the options, I knew I would get a plate.

Steak plate-
Well-done strips of beef w/WaBa sauce, salad, choice of white or brown rice & an orange for dessert.  A hearty & healthy meal, the WaBa sauce wasn't cloyingly sweet.  While I much prefer it rare to medium-rare, the beef was good.  I loved the fact that brown rice is available at no additional charge.  The salad provided the greens & roughage, while the tart orange gave a nice ending to my non-fried meal.

A condiment bar let's diners load up on Waba sauce (teriyaki & hot), green onions, pickled carrots & jalapenos, and lemon slices.  Being an onion lover, I availed myself of a heaping helping of green onions, of which I basically used to make a green onion salad on top of my steak plate.  Good for you & crunchy to boot!  Other menu options include salmon, shrimp & tofu.

The sole unisex restroom was clean & tidy.  Service was good.  The cashier was friendly & seemed to be happy to be working there, which is refreshing.  Attitude is everything!

Parking is in a private lot shared by a bank, United Boardshop, Glory Days Sports Bar & other businesses.

WaBa Grill offers up healthy & tasty meals in a pleasant environment.  While not taking the crown from my beloved Yoshinoya, what WaBa has going for it is that brown rice is available at no additional charge, minimal wait & the food was filling & satisfying.  I enjoyed my meal while listening to Train, LifeHouse & the Red Hot Chili Peppers on the house speakers.  We received coupons for a free chicken bowl with purchase of a plate & free fountain drink with purchase of a bowl/plate.  I'll definitely stop by soon to redeem them whenever my tastebuds scream "WaBa, WaBa", again.

Highly recommend!
NOMNOMNOMNOMNOMNOMNOMNOMNOMNOMNOM</Review>

< Review>
This place is awesome! Even at peak dinner hours there is always room to sit down and eat. Their go to burger, the Hook Burger, is actually very well priced considering its size and preparation. You could easily pay an extra $5 for this at a fancier place.
Another notable mention is the small brand fountain sodas they have available with real sugar. Try them out, I especially enjoyed the ginger ale.</Review>

<username>Ashton Sherer</username>< Review>
I love Hook Burger. It doesn't matter which one I go to. There's consistent quality and delicious flavors at every location. This place has a nice seating area outside that is very relaxed. Perfect for a hot summer day. I usually get the hickory burger and sweet potato fries. Not at all what I'd refer to as healthy, but it certainly is tasty and filling. It's worth mentioning they do have salads as well, if you want something lighter. The people who work here are total sweethearts too. You should definitely give it a try if you're looking for a new favorite burger place.< /Review>

< review>
Ive tried this spot various times from past experiences sometimes the burger was juicy, some of the other times it was dry and the fries were as hard as rock basically. A decent meal your looking to spend around $10. Today I went on my lunch break and man today the burger was super savory, I ordered the Maui burger and I added bacon as well with some fries it came out to be around $12 no drink included. It was really well made, overall the burger was delicious, but for the price its somewhat ridiculous. I might as well go to in-n-out and order a double double combo for $8 and be completely satisfied. This place is good on a good day (depending the cook on whether he makes it dry or not), but in my opinion not $12 good. Pricing is unreasonably high.</review>

< text>
This burger place used to be awesome, but recently, the quality of the food has gone down.  The past 3 out of 4 times I've gone, the bread has been rock hard, as if toasted before the meat and allowed to harden, and the meat has been hard as well, clearly way over-cooked.  It leads to a less than satisfying burger.   Every time, it was the Pretzel Burger.

I'm not sure what's happened or change, but it has been a rapid change from great burgers to very mediocre ones.  I will give this place a break, as it simply is no longer the quality burger it was when it opened.

Whoever the owner is needs to look into it, as whoever/whatever is roasting the bread is giving out rock hard bread and whoever is now cooking the meat, is going overboard on them being well done.  When you get the same crappy burger, three out of four times, from May 2015 to September 2015, it isn't by accident.

Until this changes, I can no longer recommend Hook Burger...'tis a shame.</text>

< text>
Nice clean Restaurant. Staff was an A+ in my book...i was greeted upon entering and provided a menu to look at.

There are plenty of tables to sit at or you can sit by the ordering area on stoll chairs which are near the TVs.

The cashier was very nice and friendly.

I ordered the hickory burger with cheddar cheese. I waited about 10 minutes for my  order.

Tip: they sell beer and have a beer of the month for all of ya'll beer drinkers ...lol!

Will be back one day to try other items.< /text>
